<script>
    googletag.cmd.push(function() {
        for (var adSlot in advertisingSlots) {
            var ad = advertisingSlots[adSlot];
            var mqStr = '';
            // Skip loop if the property is from prototype
            if (!advertisingSlots.hasOwnProperty(adSlot)) {
                continue;
            }
            // Skip if already defined
            if (ad.slot) {
                continue;
            }
            // Construct media query
            if (ad.minWidh) {
                mqStr = '(min-width: ' + ad.minWidh + 'px)';
            }
            if (ad.maxWidth) {
                if (mqStr !== '') {
                    mqStr += ' and ';
                }
                mqStr += '(max-width: ' + ad.maxWidth + 'px)';
            }
            if (!mqStr || Modernizr.mq(mqStr)) {
                ad.slot = googletag.defineSlot(ad.path, ad.size, 'div-gpt-ad-' + adSlot)
                    .addService(googletag.pubads())
                    .setTargeting(ad.targetingKey, [ad.targetingValue]);
            }
        }
        // A-start
        googletag.pubads().disableInitialLoad();
        googletag.pubads().collapseEmptyDivs();
        googletag.pubads().enableVideoAds();
        var crtg_split = (crtg_content || '').split(';');
        var pubads = googletag.pubads();
        for (var i = 1; i < crtg_split.length; i++) {
            pubads.setTargeting("" + (crtg_split[i - 1].split('='))[0] + "", "" + (crtg_split[i - 1].split('='))[1] + "");
        }
        googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();
        googletag.enableServices();
        // A-end
    });
</script>

<script async="async" src="https://www.googletagservices.com/tag/js/gpt.js" type="text/javascript"></script>
<script type="text/javascript">
    var advertisingShow = function(id, slot, bodyClass) {
        googletag.cmd.push(function() {
            googletag.pubads().addEventListener('slotRenderEnded', function(event) {
                if (bodyClass && slot && event.slot === slot && !event.isEmpty) {
                    var body = document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0];
                    var classes = body.className.split(' ');
                    var alreadyAdded = false;
                    classes.forEach(function(className) {
                        if (className === bodyClass) {
                            alreadyAdded = true;
                        }
                    });
                    if (alreadyAdded) {
                        return;
                    }
                    classes.push(bodyClass);
                    body.className = classes.join(' ');
                }
            });
            googletag.display(id);
            // Refresh (Ignore if Prebid is present. Refresh is done by it)
            if (typeof pbjs === 'undefined') {
                googletag.pubads().refresh([slot]);
            }
        });
    };
</script>
